  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:right;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Exhibit 99.1</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><img src="img247042425_0.jpg" alt="img247042425_0.jpg" style="width:136px;height:68px;">&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.4950000000000003;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.4950000000000003;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Athira Pharma Reports Third Quarter 2021 Financial Results and Business Update</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> &#x2013; Completed enrollment of ACT-AD trial with topline data expected in the first half of 2022; LIFT-AD is actively recruiting with topline data expected by the end of 2022 &#x2013;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">&#x2013; Presented program updates and baseline data from ATH-1017&#x2019;s ongoing Phase 2 and Phase 2/3 clinical trials at the 2021 CTAD conference &#x2013;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">BOTHELL, Wash., November 10, 2021</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> &#x2014; </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Athira Pharma, Inc.</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> (NASDAQ: ATHA), a late clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on developing small molecules to restore neuronal health and stop neurodegeneration, today reported its financial results for the third quarter ended September 30, 2021, and provided an update on the company&#x2019;s operations.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#x201c;We remained focused on our development efforts during the third quarter of 2021, and</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">our initiatives remain on track as we enter a potentially transformative phase with multiple near-term clinical events,&#x201d; said Mark Litton, Ph.D., President and Chief Executive Officer at Athira. &#x201c;The completion of enrollment in our ACT-AD trial is an important step forward in advancing the development of ATH-1017 with the goal of improving the lives for those suffering from Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease. We look forward to sharing topline results from this Phase 2 trial in the first half of 2022. In parallel, our LIFT-AD trial is actively recruiting with topline results targeted by the end of 2022, and SHAPE, our Phase 2 trial for patients with Parkinson&#x2019;s disease dementia or dementia with Lewy bodies, is expected to initiate later this year. As we evaluate the year ahead, we are well-funded for the continued execution of our planned clinical development and look forward to advancing our pipeline of small molecule therapeutics.&#x201d;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Clinical Development and Upcoming Milestones</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">ATH-1017: </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">A small molecule therapeutic specifically designed to enhance the activity of hepatocyte growth factor (HGF) and its receptor, MET, to impact neurodegeneration and regenerate brain tissue. ATH-1017 is currently being evaluated in two randomized, double-blind, placebo-controlled trials, LIFT-AD and ACT-AD, designed to evaluate the safety and efficacy of the investigational therapeutic in individuals with mild-to-moderate Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">Recent Advancements</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.25in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.25in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">ACT-AD Phase 2 trial:</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> Completed enrollment with topline data expected in the first half of 2022. This Phase 2 randomized, double-blind, placebo-controlled, parallel-group study of ATH-1017 in patients with mild-to-moderate Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease has enrolled 77 subjects across 14 sites in the United States and Australia. The primary endpoint for ACT-AD is Event-Related-Potential (ERP) P300 latency, a functional measure of working </font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.25in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;visibility:hidden;display:inline-block;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.25in;"></font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">memory processing speed, and secondary endpoints measuring cognition, function and behavior.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">  </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.25in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.25in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">2021 Clinical Trials on Alzheimer&#x2019;s Disease Conference (CTAD): </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Provided program updates and baseline data from ATH-1017&#x2019;s ongoing Phase 2 and Phase 2/3 clinical trials in an oral presentation at CTAD.</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;"> </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.25in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.25in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Open Label Extension Study for LIFT-AD and ACT-AD trials of ATH-1017: </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">The study is ongoing and was initiated in June 2021. Following completion of the 26-week treatment period during the LIFT-AD or ACT-AD trials, study participants may elect to continue on the open label extension and receive treatment with ATH-1017 at the high dose (70 mg/day) for up to an additional 26 weeks.</font></div></div>
  <p style="margin-left:13.333%;text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">Upcoming Milestones</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.25in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.25in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">LIFT-AD Phase 2/3 trial</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> of ATH-1017 in patients with mild-to-moderate Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease is actively recruiting, with top-line data expected by the end of 2022.</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.25in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.25in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">SHAPE Phase 2 trial</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> of ATH-1017 in patients with Parkinson&#x2019;s disease dementia or dementia with Lewy bodies is anticipated to initiate by the end of 2021.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Pipeline Advancements</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">ATH-1020: </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">A</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">novel, small molecule therapeutic designed to be an orally available, once-daily treatment. ATH-1020 is intended to enhance the HGF/MET system and distribute to the central nervous system as a potential candidate for neuropsychiatric indications.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">Upcoming Milestone</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.25in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.25in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">IND filing expected by end of 2021. </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">IND-enabling studies are proceeding for ATH-1020. Athira is targeting an IND submission to the U.S. Food and Drug Administration (FDA) by the end of 2021. </font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Recent Corporate Event</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.25in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.25in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Educational webinar:</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> On November 5, 2021, the company hosted an educational webinar on the clinical applications of ERP P300 latency as a functional measure of working memory processing speed, as well as its correlation to cognition. The webinar featured a discussion with John Michael Olichney, M.D., a board-certified behavioral neurologist and Professor of Neurology at UC Davis Health; Hans Moebius, M.D., Ph.D., Chief Medical Officer of Athira; and Kevin Church, Ph.D., EVP, Research at Athira. An archived replay of the webinar can be accessed from the investors&#x2019; section of the Athira website at </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">https://investors.athira.com/news-and-events/events-and-presentations</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>

  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.25in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.25in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Cash Position</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">. Cash, cash equivalents and investments were $339.4 million as of September 30, 2021, compared to $268.2 million as of December 31, 2020.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&#160;</font></p>

  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">

  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.25in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.25in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Research and Development (R&amp;D) Expenses</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">. R&amp;D expenses were $10.7 million for the quarter ended September 30, 2021, as compared to $5.8 million for the same quarter in 2020.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.25in;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;display:inline-block;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.25in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">General and Administrative (G&amp;A) Expenses. </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">G&amp;A expenses were $7.1 million for the quarter ended September 30, 2021, as compared to $1.6 million for the same quarter in 2020.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>

Net loss was $15.7 million, or $0.42 per share basic and diluted, for the quarter ended September 30, 2021, compared to a net loss of $8.5 million, or $1.12 per share basic and diluted, for the same quarter in 2020.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.4950000000000003;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">About Athira Pharma, Inc.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.4950000000000003;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Athira, headquartered in the Seattle area, is a late clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on developing small molecules to restore neuronal health and stop neurodegeneration. Athira aims to provide rapid cognitive improvement and alter the course of neurological diseases with our novel mechanism of action. Athira is currently advancing its lead therapeutic candidate, ATH-1017, a novel small molecule for Alzheimer&#x2019;s and Parkinson&#x2019;s disease dementia. For more information, visit </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">www.athira.com</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">. You can also follow Athira on </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Facebook</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">, </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">LinkedIn</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> and @athirapharma on </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Twitter</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> and </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Instagram</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">.</font></p>
